### [257] [CFEAR-Teach-and-Repeat: Fast and Accurate Radar-only Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06501)
*Maximilian Hilger,Daniel Adolfsson,Ralf Becker,Henrik Andreasson,Achim J. Lilienthal*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: CFEAR-TR是一种基于单线雷达的teach-and-repeat定位系统，能在恶劣天气下提升自动导航定位的准确性与鲁棒性，相比现有方法精度显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在恶劣天气下，传统基于光学传感器的定位系统容易失效，因此需要一种对恶劣环境鲁棒且易于部署的高精度定位方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于单旋转雷达的teach-and-repeat本地化管线，通过将实时雷达扫描与预先记录的地图扫描、以及最近的关键帧联合对齐，提升定位精度。雷达数据以稀疏定向表面点描述，并通过位姿图结构存储与遍历。

Result: 在Boreas数据集测试集上，CFEAR-TR的定位精度达到0.117米和0.096°，相较于现有方法提升高达63%，运行速度达29 Hz。

Conclusion: 该方法显著提高了恶劣天气下自动导航的定位性能，部分缩小了与激光雷达定位精度的差距，并已开源C++实现。

Abstract: Reliable localization in prior maps is essential for autonomous navigation, particularly under adverse weather, where optical sensors may fail. We present CFEAR-TR, a teach-and-repeat localization pipeline using a single spinning radar, which is designed for easily deployable, lightweight, and robust navigation in adverse conditions. Our method localizes by jointly aligning live scans to both stored scans from the teach mapping pass, and to a sliding window of recent live keyframes. This ensures accurate and robust pose estimation across different seasons and weather phenomena. Radar scans are represented using a sparse set of oriented surface points, computed from Doppler-compensated measurements. The map is stored in a pose graph that is traversed during localization. Experiments on the held-out test sequences from the Boreas dataset show that CFEAR-TR can localize with an accuracy as low as 0.117 m and 0.096°, corresponding to improvements of up to 63% over the previous state of the art, while running efficiently at 29 Hz. These results substantially narrow the gap to lidar-level localization, particularly in heading estimation. We make the C++ implementation of our work available to the community.

</details>


### [258] [SG-DOR: Learning Scene Graphs with Direction-Conditioned Occlusion Reasoning for Pepper Plants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06512)
*Rohit Menon,Niklas Mueller-Goldingen,Sicong Pan,Gokul Krishna Chenchani,Maren Bennewitz*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种新颖的基于方向条件遮挡推理的场景图方法（SG-DOR），能更好地解析茂密作物冠层下的果实及其遮挡关系，支持机器人自主采摘决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在密集作物冠层下，机器人采摘不仅依赖于几何位置信息，还需要理解和识别哪些器官（如叶片）会从特定方向遮挡目标果实，这对精准高效的采摘尤为关键。

Method: 提出SG-DOR框架：以实例分割后的器官点云为输入，推理生成场景图，编码果实附着关系及方向条件下的遮挡情况。此外，引入一个遮挡排序任务，对目标果实的候选遮挡叶片按采摘方向评分与排序，并设计了具备针对果实的叶片集合注意力和联合层级聚合的方向感知图神经网络架构。

Result: 在多植株合成辣椒数据集上，该方法遮挡预测指标（F1=0.73，NDCG@3=0.85）及附着推理结果（边F1=0.83）均优于强基线，为后续机器人操作规划提供了结构化的关系信号。

Conclusion: SG-DOR方法能显著提升复杂作物环境下器官关系识别和遮挡推理，为精准机器人采摘策略奠定基础。

Abstract: Robotic harvesting in dense crop canopies requires effective interventions that depend not only on geometry, but also on explicit, direction-conditioned relations identifying which organs obstruct a target fruit. We present SG-DOR (Scene Graphs with Direction-Conditioned Occlusion Reasoning), a relational framework that, given instance-segmented organ point clouds, infers a scene graph encoding physical attachments and direction-conditioned occlusion. We introduce an occlusion ranking task for retrieving and ranking candidate leaves for a target fruit and approach direction, and propose a direction-aware graph neural architecture with per-fruit leaf-set attention and union-level aggregation. Experiments on a multi-plant synthetic pepper dataset show improved occlusion prediction (F1=0.73, NDCG@3=0.85) and attachment inference (edge F1=0.83) over strong ablations, yielding a structured relational signal for downstream intervention planning.

</details>


### [259] [Underactuated multimodal jumping robot for extraterrestrial exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06525)
*Neil R. Wagner,Justin K. Yim*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种带有滚动和跳跃功能的欠驱动单足机器人，仅使用两个反作用轮和一个腿部驱动器，实现多模态运动，适用于低重力环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在低重力星体表面进行多模态移动的可能性，设计一种结构简单、体积小巧、执行器数量极少、但能灵活适应不同环境和地形的机器人。

Method: 机器人结构采用单足设计，仅配备两个反作用轮，利用滚动和跳跃实现移动。通过两个控制器分别实现地面时的平衡与跳跃方向调整（平衡控制器），和飞行时的空间姿态调整以优化落地（空中重新定向控制器）。通过简单的运动模式切换，根据地形灵活采用滚动、跳跃、自我翻正等能力。

Result: 在0.33米、1.25千克的小型化结构下，机器人使用三个执行器实现了滚动、目标跳跃与着陆、自我翻正等复杂动作。系统能根据环境顺利切换运动模式，应对多样化地形。

Conclusion: 证明了极简结构的单足机器人能够通过多模态运动适应复杂环境，为在低重力天体上实现灵活、可靠的机器人探测提供了一种新方向。

Abstract: We present a rolling and jumping underactuated monopedal robot designed to explore multimodal locomotion on low-gravity bodies. It uses only two reaction wheels to control its spatial orientation with two controllers: a balancing controller which can aim the robot's jump direction on the ground, and an aerial reorientation controller which can aim the robot's leg for landing after flight. We demonstrate rolling, targeted jumping and landing, and self-righting using only three actuators total, keeping system size to 0.33m and 1.25kg. Simple switching between locomotion modes enables the system to deal with differing landscapes and environmental conditions.

</details>


### [260] [Unified Learning of Temporal Task Structure and Action Timing for Bimanual Robot Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06538)
*Christian Dreher,Patrick Dormanns,Andre Meixner,Tamim Asfour*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种能够同时学习符号（高层）和子符号（低层）时序任务约束的方法，并基于人类演示生成适用于双手机器人操作的可执行、具备具体时间参数的任务计划。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法只能在高层任务规划和低层动作同步中单独处理时序结构，无法将高层符号关系和低层具体时间参数结合，导致机器人双手协调操作存在脱节。本文旨在弥合这一差距，使机器人能更自然地模仿人类的协调动作。

Method: 1) 设计了三维时序表示方法，用多元高斯混合模型（GMM）描述动作间的低层时序关系；2) 基于DPLL算法搜索所有无矛盾的Allen时序关系分配，实现高层任务模式的多样性表示和排序；3) 优化规划系统，将符号与子符号级约束结合，输出具备具体执行时间参数的任务计划。

Result: 在多个数据集上验证，所提方法生成的双手操作任务计划在时序参数上明显更接近人类演示结果，优于以最具代表性的单次演示作为基线的方法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的融合符号与子符号时序约束的学习与规划方法，有效提升了机器人双手操作任务在任务计划时序上的拟人性和准确性，为复杂人类技能机器人模仿与执行提供了新思路。

Abstract: Temporal task structure is fundamental for bimanual manipulation: a robot must not only know that one action precedes or overlaps another, but also when each action should occur and how long it should take. While symbolic temporal relations enable high-level reasoning about task structure and alternative execution sequences, concrete timing parameters are equally essential for coordinating two hands at the execution level. Existing approaches address these two levels in isolation, leaving a gap between high-level task planning and low-level movement synchronization. This work presents an approach for learning both symbolic and subsymbolic temporal task constraints from human demonstrations and deriving executable, temporally parametrized plans for bimanual manipulation. Our contributions are (i) a 3-dimensional representation of timings between two actions with methods based on multivariate Gaussian Mixture Models to represent temporal relationships between actions on a subsymbolic level, (ii) a method based on the Davis-Putnam-Logemann-Loveland (DPLL) algorithm that finds and ranks all contradiction-free assignments of Allen relations to action pairs, representing different modes of a task, and (iii) an optimization-based planning system that combines the identified symbolic and subsymbolic temporal task constraints to derive temporally parametrized plans for robot execution. We evaluate our approach on several datasets, demonstrating that our method generates temporally parametrized plans closer to human demonstrations than the most characteristic demonstration baseline.

</details>


### [261] [Uncertainty-Aware Adaptive Dynamics For Underwater Vehicle-Manipulator Robots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06548)
*Edward Morgan,Nenyi K Dadson,Corina Barbalata*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出了一种针对水下机器人-机械臂系统的不确定性自适应动力学建模方法，实现了快速准确的参数估计和可靠的动态预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水下机器人-机械臂系统由于流体动力影响导致参数时变，现有动力学模型难以同时兼顾适应性、不确定性量化和物理可实现性，影响系统的建模精度和控制可靠性。

Method: 提出线性参数化的不确定性自适应动力学模型，引入凸物理一致性约束，通过滑动时间窗估计法(Moving Horizon Estimation)进行参数在线估计，确保惯性、阻尼、摩擦和静水力的物理可实现性，并量化参数进化过程中的不确定性。

Result: 在BlueROV2 Heavy水下机器人及4自由度机械臂实验中，动力学参数快速收敛且预测具高准确性，机械臂动力学拟合R2高达0.88-0.98，系统运动关键自由度（如推进、升沉、横滚）均可高保真重现。与固定参数模型相比，各自由度的MAE和RMSE均显著降低，单步计算耗时中位数0.023秒，满足在线应用需求。

Conclusion: 所提方法能获得物理合理、具有高可信度的动力学参数和置信区间，实现水下环境中更为可靠的前馈控制与动态仿真，具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: Accurate and adaptive dynamic models are critical for underwater vehicle-manipulator systems where hydrodynamic effects induce time-varying parameters. This paper introduces a novel uncertainty-aware adaptive dynamics model framework that remains linear in lumped vehicle and manipulator parameters, and embeds convex physical consistency constraints during online estimation. Moving horizon estimation is used to stack horizon regressors, enforce realizable inertia, damping, friction, and hydrostatics, and quantify uncertainty from parameter evolution. Experiments on a BlueROV2 Heavy with a 4-DOF manipulator demonstrate rapid convergence and calibrated predictions. Manipulator fits achieve R2 = 0.88 to 0.98 with slopes near unity, while vehicle surge, heave, and roll are reproduced with good fidelity under stronger coupling and noise. Median solver time is approximately 0.023 s per update, confirming online feasibility. A comparison against a fixed parameter model shows consistent reductions in MAE and RMSE across degrees of freedom. Results indicate physically plausible parameters and confidence intervals with near 100% coverage, enabling reliable feedforward control and simulation in underwater environments.

</details>


### [262] [Fly360: Omnidirectional Obstacle Avoidance within Drone View](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.06573)
*Xiangkai Zhang,Dizhe Zhang,WenZhuo Cao,Zhaoliang Wan,Yingjie Niu,Lu Qi,Xu Yang,Zhiyong Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种用于全景无人机的全方位障碍物规避方法Fly360，实现了无人机在任意方向来障碍物的环境下稳定避障，且优于传统仅依赖前视传感器的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前无人机避障方法大多依赖于有限视角的传感器，难以适应需360°空间感知、运动方向与机头不一致的复杂场景。为提升无人机的空间智能和安全性，亟需发展能够全方位避障的新方法。

Method: 作者首次探讨了无人机需全方位避障的场景，搭建了包含三种代表性飞行任务的基准测试，并提出Fly360方法：包括感知-决策两阶段流程。在感知阶段，输入全景RGB图像并生成深度图作为中间表征；决策阶段利用轻量级策略网络输出机体速度指令。引入了固定随机偏航训练策略以提升泛化能力。

Result: 在大量仿真和真实世界飞行实验中，Fly360均可实现稳定的全方位避障，并在所有测试任务上显著优于仅用前视传感器的基线方法。

Conclusion: Fly360显著提升了无人机的全景感知和空间避障能力，验证了全景输入及感知-决策两阶段流程的有效性，为无人机在复杂空间环境中的应用提供了新思路。

Abstract: Obstacle avoidance in unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs), as a fundamental capability, has gained increasing attention with the growing focus on spatial intelligence. However, current obstacle-avoidance methods mainly depend on limited field-of-view sensors and are ill-suited for UAV scenarios which require full-spatial awareness when the movement direction differs from the UAV's heading. This limitation motivates us to explore omnidirectional obstacle avoidance for panoramic drones with full-view perception. We first study an under explored problem setting in which a UAV must generate collision-free motion in environments with obstacles from arbitrary directions, and then construct a benchmark that consists of three representative flight tasks. Based on such settings, we propose Fly360, a two-stage perception-decision pipeline with a fixed random-yaw training strategy. At the perception stage, panoramic RGB observations are input and converted into depth maps as a robust intermediate representation. For the policy network, it is lightweight and used to output body-frame velocity commands from depth inputs. Extensive simulation and real-world experiments demonstrate that Fly360 achieves stable omnidirectional obstacle avoidance and outperforms forward-view baselines across all tasks. Our model is available at https://zxkai.github.io/fly360/

</details>
